#line: 6. Massachusetts. I suppose you could say I'm coming around on UMass. Or you could say I'm very rapidly transitioning from my role as someone who allows tempo-free statistics to aid much of my fickle eyeballs' analysis into someone who must acknowledge the cold realpolitik of NCAA tournament qualification. (It is kind of what I do around here .) Either way, the fact of the matter is that for as utterly mediocre as UMass' per-possessions numbers tell me the Minutemen are, and for as rarely as I've been impressed when I've watched them this season, their at-large profile is such that they have a pretty good chance of getting into the NCAA tournament. It's pretty strange: This is a team that isn't truly bad at anything (save 3-point shooting) but excels at nothing (save perhaps field-goal defense, and UMass has gotten more more and more stops in A-10 play). But its RPI and schedule numbers and lack of truly bad losses have it in position to lay claim to a bid if it can see this thing through. In a league full of confusion, there is something to be said for that.

San Antonio has won a league-best 41 games and Oklahoma City is battling the Spurs for the top seed in the Western Conference. The Thunder have won four consecutive games as they face a Utah squad that has lost two straight contests after losing to the Sacramento Kings on Saturday.The Jazz are currently seventh in the Western Conference playoff race. Utah has lost back-to-back games with the first of those being a rare home loss. The Jazz fell to the Chicago Bulls on Friday to drop to 19-6 at home. Oklahoma City clobbered the Phoenix Suns twice by a combined 59 points and Sunday's 97-69 victory marked just the third time in 14 games that the Thunder didn't reach 100 points. Oklahoma City is 16-9 on the road.TV: 9 p.m. ET, Fox Sports Oklahoma, ROOT (Utah)ABOUT THE THUNDER (39-12): Oklahoma City has won each game by more than 20 points during the current winning streak, with the average victory being 25.3 points. The Thunder have allowed an average of 88.5 points during the stretch as the defensive performance has been as impressive as the typically solid offense. "Defense first," All-Star forward Kevin Durant said. "These last two or three games have been great for us on the defensive end, setting the tone. We have to keep it up." Guard Russell Westbrook had 23 points, 13 rebounds, eight assists and seven steals when the Thunder beat the Jazz 106-94 on Nov. 30.ABOUT THE JAZZ (28-24): Utah certainly wants to avoid a third straight loss with the All-Star break looming.
